(* References:
1. KayeLabyOnline2005: "Tables of Physical & Chemical Constants" (16th edition 1995), Kaye & Laby Online. Version 1.0, www.kayelaby.npl.co.uk, 2005.
2. Larminie2003: J. Larminie and A. Dicks, Fuel Cell Systems Explained, New York: John Wiley & Sons, 2003.
 3. McBride2002: B.J. McBride, M.J. Zehe, and S. Gordon, "NASA Glenn Coefficients for Calculating Thermodynamic Properties of Individual Species," NASA report TP-2002-211556, 2002.
 4. Moran2004: M.J. Moran and H.N.Shapiro, Fundamentals of Engineering Thermodynamics, 5th ed. Hoboken, NJ: John Wiley & Sons, Inc., 2004.
 5. Moran2008: M.J. Moran and H.N.Shapiro, Fundamentals of Engineering Thermodynamics, 6th ed. Hoboken, NJ: John Wiley & Sons, Inc., 2008.
 6. NIST2009: National Institute of Standards and Technology (NIST), "Fundamental Physical Constants --- Complete Listing", http://physics.nist.gov/cuu/Constants/Table/allascii.txt, accessed June 26 2009.
*)
SetOptions[Plot,
Axes->False,
Frame->True,
FrameStyle->Directive[Thickness[0.0022]],
PlotStyle->{
Directive[Blue,Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Green,Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Red,Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Cyan,Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Magenta,Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Yellow,Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Black,Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Blue,Thickness[0.002]]},
ImageSize->{(1+Sqrt[5])/2,1}*500, (* Golden ratio *) 
BaseStyle->{FontFamily->"Helvetica",FontSize->13}]; (* Default plot options *)
(* 6/17/11: The last PlotStyle is the same as the first.  Otherwise, where there is only one line in a plot,the PlotStyle in the legend doesn't seem to match the PlotStyle in the plot. *)
(* 6/17/11: Unfortunately, the dashing of the lines in the legend doesn't match the dashing of the lines in the plot, so this can't be used:
PlotStyle->{Directive[Blue,Dashing[{1,0}],Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Green,Dashing[{0.015,0.015}],Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Red,Dashing[{0.005,0.005}],Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Cyan,Dashing[{0.015,0.010,0.005,0.010}],Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Magenta,Dashing[{1,0}],Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Yellow,Dashing[{0.005,0.005}],Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Black,Dashing[{0.015,0.010,0.005,0.010}],Thickness[0.002]],
Directive[Blue,Dashing[{1,0}],Thickness[0.002]]}
*)
(* 10/2/11: Updated the formatting to match that of matplotlib. *)
(* 10/2/11: ImageSize needs to be large enough so that the PNGs are exported with sufficient quality. *)
(* Custom method for adding labels (modified from http://www.mathkb.com/Uwe/Forum.aspx/mathematica/16793/Legends-for-Plot-s-solution) *)
(* This is necessary since it is otherwise difficult to set the width of lines in the legend to match those of the plot. 
Unfortunately, however, it does not allow the legend to be placed within the plot frame. *)
LineStylesFromTooltips[plot_Graphics]:=Cases[plot,Tooltip[{s__,l_Point|l_Line},tt_]:>
Grid[{{
Switch[
Head@l,Point,
Graphics[
Flatten[{s,Point@{0,0}}],
ImageSize->{4,8},
AspectRatio->8/4,
ImagePadding->0],
Line,
Graphics[
Flatten[{s,
Thickness[0.06],(* Based on inspection, this matches a thickness of 0.002 in the PlotStyle option. *)
Line[{{0,0},{1,0}}]}],
ImageSize->{24,8},
AspectRatio->8/24,
ImagePadding->0]],
tt}}],
Infinity];
LineLegendFromTooltips[plot_Graphics]:=Labeled[
plot,
Style[
Column[LineStylesFromTooltips[plot]],
"TR",
FontFamily->"Helvetica",
FontSize->13,
ShowStringCharacters->False],
Right] (* Place the legend to the right of the plot. *)
(* This can be added within the call to Column[] in order to add a border around the legend:
  Frame->True,
     FrameStyle->Directive[Thickness[1.2]] *)
(* Example of usage:
LineLegendFromTooltips[Plot[{Tooltip[x,"x"],Tooltip[x^2,"x^2"]},{x,0,3}]] *)
(* Units *)
(* See FCSys/Units.mo. *)
Us =1; (* second *)
Um =1*^-3; (* meter *)
US=1*^3; (* siemen *)
UWb=1*^-3; (* weber *)
UC=UWb*US; (* coulomb; C can't be used because it is a protected symbol in Mathematica. *)
UV:=UWb/Us; (* volt *)
UJ:=UV*UC; (* joule *)
Umol:=96485.3399*UC; (* mol; from "Faraday constant," NIST2009 *)
UK:=8.314472*UJ/Umol; (* kelvin *)
USv:=(Um/Us)^2; (* Sv *)
Ukg:=UJ/USv; (* kg *)

(* Dummy variables *)
a:={a1,a2,a3,a4,a5,a6,a7}
b:={b1,b2}
(* McBride2002 gas data for e^- over the lower temperature range (200 K to 1000 K) *)
meminus:=5.48579903*^-7Ukg/Umol (* Mass per unit number of particles *)
aeminus:={0,0,2.5,0,0,0,0} (* {Sv^-2, Sv^-1, 1, Sv, Sv^2, Sv^3, Sv^4}; Coefficients for dimensionless heat capacity (molar heat capacity per gas constant) at 1 bar *)
beminus:={-745.375UK/meminus,-11.72081224}+{aeminus[[2]],aeminus[[3]]}Log[meminus/UK]  (* {Sv, 1}; Integration constants for enthalpy and entropy *)
hf0eminus:=0USv (* Enthalpy of formation at 298.15 K *)
Deltah0eminus:=11297220270.20738USv (* Enthalpy at 298 K minus the enthalpy at 0 K *)
(* Units and descriptions are the same for the other species below. *)
(* McBride2002 gas data for H over the lower temperature range (200 to 1000 K) *)
mH:=0.00100794Ukg/Umol
aH:={0,0,2.5,0,0,0,0}
bH:={25473.70801UK/mH,-0.446682853}+{aH[[2]],aH[[3]]}Log[mH/UK] 
hf0H:=216281552.4733615USv
Deltah0H:=6148608.052066591USv
(* McBride2002 gas data for H^+ over the lower temperature range (200 to 1000 K) *)
mHplus:=0.0010073914Ukg/Umol
aHplus:={0,0,2.5,0,0,0,0}
bHplus:={184021.4877UK/mHplus,-1.140646644}+{aHplus[[2]],aHplus[[3]]}Log[mHplus/UK] 
hf0Hplus:=1524974233.450872USv
Deltah0Hplus:=6151956.429248851USv
(* McBride2002 gas data for H^- over the lower temperature range (200 to 1000 K) *)
mHminus:=0.0010084886*Ukg/Umol
aHminus:={0,0,2.5,0,0,0,0}
bHminus:={15976.15494UK/mHminus,-1.139013868}+{aHminus[[2]],aHminus[[3]]}Log[mHminus/UK] 
hf0Hminus:=137861080.4326395USv
Deltah0Hminus:=6145263.317800519USv
(* McBride2002 gas data for Subscript[H, 2] over the lower temperature range (200 to 1000 K) *)
mH2:=0.001501588Ukg/Umol
aH2:={40783.2321(mH2/UK)^-2,-800.918604(mH2/UK)^-1,8.21470201,-0.01269714457mH2/UK,1.753605076*^-5(mH2/UK)^2,-1.20286027*^-8(mH2/UK)^3,3.36809349*^-12(mH2/UK)^4}
bH2:={2682.484665UK/mH2,-30.43788844}+{aH2[[2]],aH2[[3]]}Log[mH2/UK]
hf0H2:=0USv
Deltah0H2:=4200697.46215052USv
(* McBride2002 gas data for Subscript[H, 2]O over the lower temperature range (200 to 1000 K) *)
mH2O:=0.01801528Ukg/Umol
aH2O:={-39479.6083(mH2O/UK)^-2,575.573102(mH2O/UK)^-1,0.931782653,0.00722271286mH2O/UK,-7.34255737*^-6(mH2O/UK)^2,4.95504349*^-9(mH2O/UK)^3,-1.336933246*^-12(mH2O/UK)^4}
bH2O:={-33039.7431UK/mH2O,17.24205775}+{aH2O[[2]],aH2O[[3]]}Log[mH2O/UK] 
hf0H2O:=-13423382.8172529USv
Deltah0H2O:=549760.647628014USv
(* McBride2002 liquid data for Subscript[H, 2]O over the lower temperature range (273.15 to 373.15 K) *)
aH2Ol:={1.326371304*^9(mH2O/UK)^-2,-2.448295388*^7(mH2O/UK)^-1,1.879428776*^5,-7.678995050*^2mH2O/UK,1.761556813(mH2O/UK)^2 ,-2.151167128*^-3(mH2O/UK)^3,1.092570813*^-6(mH2O/UK)^4}
bH2Ol:={1.101760476*^8UK/mH2O,-9.779700970*^5}+{aH2Ol[[2]],aH2Ol[[3]]}Log[mH2O/UK] 
hf0H2Ol:=-285830.000USv 
Deltah0H2Ol:=13278.000USv
(* McBride2002 gas data for Subscript[H, 3] O^+ over the lower temperature range (200 to 1000 K) *)
mH3Oplus:=0.0190226714Ukg/Umol
aH3Oplus:={-64476.4015(mH3Oplus/UK)^-2,1181.817922(mH3Oplus/UK)^-1,-3.80189306,0.02220628313mH3Oplus/UK,-2.445343237*^-5(mH3Oplus/UK)^2,1.573297747*^-8(mH3Oplus/UK)^3,-4.15883641*^-12(mH3Oplus/UK)^4}
bH3Oplus:={65306.1332UK/mH3Oplus,42.8272313}+{aH3Oplus[[2]],aH3Oplus[[3]]}*Log[mH3Oplus/UK] 
hf0H3Oplus:=31436173.57549476USv
Deltah0H3Oplus:=6148608.052066591USv
(* McBride2002 gas data for Subscript[O, 2] over the lower temperature range (200 to 1000 K) *)
mO2:=0.0319988Ukg/Umol
aO2:={-34255.6342(mO2/UK)^-2,484.700097(mO2/UK)^-1,1.119010961,0.00429388924mO2/UK,-6.83630052*^-7(mO2/UK)^2,-2.0233727*^-9(mO2/UK)^3,1.039040018*^-12(mO2/UK)^4}
bO2:={-3391.45487UK/mO2,18.4969947}+{aO2[[2]],aO2[[3]]}Log[mO2/UK] 
hf0O2:=0USv
Deltah0O2:=271263.422378339USv
(* Heat capacity functions at 1 bar from McBride2002 *)
(* Each is dimensionless. theta2 is temperature times number per unit mass--the square of thermal velocity. *)
cp0[theta2_]:=a[[1]]theta2^-2+a[[2]]theta2^-1+a[[3]]+a[[4]]theta2+a[[5]]theta2^2+a[[6]]theta2^3+a[[7]]theta2^4
cp0eminus[theta2_]:=aeminus[[1]]theta2^-2+aeminus[[2]]theta2^-1+aeminus[[3]]+aeminus[[4]]theta2+aeminus[[5]]theta2^2+aeminus[[6]]theta2^3+aeminus[[7]]theta2^4
cp0H[theta2_]:=aH[[1]]theta2^-2+aH[[2]]theta2^-1+aH[[3]]+aH[[4]]theta2+aH[[5]]theta2^2+aH[[6]]theta2^3+aH[[7]]theta2^4
cp0Hplus[theta2_]:=aHplus[[1]]theta2^-2+aHplus[[2]]theta2^-1+aHplus[[3]]+aHplus[[4]]theta2+aHplus[[5]]theta2^2+aHplus[[6]]theta2^3+aHplus[[7]]theta2^4
cp0Hminus[theta2_]:=aHminus[[1]]theta2^-2+aHminus[[2]]theta2^-1+aHminus[[3]]+aHminus[[4]]theta2+aHminus[[5]]theta2^2+aHminus[[6]]theta2^3+aHminus[[7]]theta2^4
cp0H2[theta2_]:=aH2[[1]]theta2^-2+aH2[[2]]theta2^-1+aH2[[3]]+aH2[[4]]theta2+aH2[[5]]theta2^2+aH2[[6]]theta2^3+aH2[[7]]theta2^4
cp0H2O[theta2_]:=aH2O[[1]]theta2^-2+aH2O[[2]]theta2^-1+aH2O[[3]]+aH2O[[4]]theta2+aH2O[[5]]theta2^2+aH2O[[6]]theta2^3+aH2O[[7]]theta2^4
cp0H2Ol[theta2_]:=aH2Ol[[1]]theta2^-2+aH2Ol[[2]]theta2^-1+aH2Ol[[3]]+aH2Ol[[4]]theta2+aH2Ol[[5]]theta2^2+aH2Ol[[6]]theta2^3+aH2Ol[[7]]theta2^4
cp0H3Oplus[theta2_]:=aH3Oplus[[1]]theta2^-2+aH3Oplus[[2]]theta2^-1+aH3Oplus[[3]]+aH3Oplus[[4]]theta2+aH3Oplus[[5]]theta2^2+aH3Oplus[[6]]theta2^3+aH3Oplus[[7]]theta2^4
cp0O2[theta2_]:=aO2[[1]]theta2^-2+aO2[[2]]theta2^-1+aO2[[3]]+aO2[[4]]theta2+aO2[[5]]theta2^2+aO2[[6]]theta2^3+aO2[[7]]theta2^4
(* Entropy functions at 1 bar *)
(* Each is dimensionless. *)
(* **What is the offset of integration and the reference temperature?  See enthalpy below. *)
s0[theta2_]:=Integrate[cp0[theta2]/theta2,theta2]
s0eminus[theta2_]:=-aeminus[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aeminus[[2]]theta2^-1+aeminus[[3]]*Log[theta2]+aeminus[[4]]theta2+aeminus[[5]]theta2^2/2+aeminus[[6]]theta2^3/3+aeminus[[7]]theta2^4/4 +beminus[[2]]
s0H[theta2_]:=-aH[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aH[[2]]theta2^-1+aH[[3]]*Log[theta2]+aH[[4]]theta2+aH[[5]]theta2^2/2+aH[[6]]theta2^3/3+aH[[7]]theta2^4/4+bH[[2]]
s0Hplus[theta2_]:=-aHplus[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aHplus[[2]]theta2^-1+aHplus[[3]]Log[theta2]+aHplus[[4]]theta2+aHplus[[5]]theta2^2/2+aHplus[[6]]theta2^3/3+aHplus[[7]]theta2^4/4+bHplus[[2]]
s0Hminus[theta2_]:=-aHminus[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aHminus[[2]]theta2^-1+aHminus[[3]]Log[theta2]+aHminus[[4]]theta2+aHminus[[5]]theta2^2/2+aHminus[[6]]theta2^3/3+aHminus[[7]]theta2^4/4+bHminus[[2]]
s0H2[theta2_]:=-aH2[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aH2[[2]]theta2^-1+aH2[[3]]Log[theta2]+aH2[[4]]theta2+aH2[[5]]theta2^2/2+aH2[[6]]theta2^3/3+aH2[[7]]theta2^4/4+bH2[[2]]
s0H2O[theta2_]:=-aH2O[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aH2O[[2]]theta2^-1+aH2O[[3]]Log[theta2]+aH2O[[4]]theta2+aH2O[[5]]theta2^2/2+aH2O[[6]]theta2^3/3+aH2O[[7]]theta2^4/4+bH2O[[2]]
s0H2Ol[theta2_]:=-aH2Ol[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aH2Ol[[2]]theta2^-1+aH2Ol[[3]]Log[theta2]+aH2Ol[[4]]theta2+aH2Ol[[5]]theta2^2/2+aH2Ol[[6]]theta2^3/3+aH2Ol[[7]]theta2^4/4+bH2Ol[[2]]
s0H3Oplus[theta2_]:=-aH3Oplus[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aH3Oplus[[2]]theta2^-1+aH3Oplus[[3]]Log[theta2]+aH3Oplus[[4]]theta2+aH3Oplus[[5]]theta2^2/2+aH3Oplus[[6]]theta2^3/3+aH3Oplus[[7]]theta2^4/4+bH3Oplus[[2]]
s0O2[theta2_]:=-aO2[[1]]theta2^-2/2-aO2[[2]]theta2^-1+aO2[[3]]Log[theta2]+aO2[[4]]theta2+aO2[[5]]theta2^2/2+aO2[[6]]theta2^3/3+aO2[[7]]theta2^4/4+bO2[[2]]
Part::partd: Part specification 0[[1]] is longer than depth of object. >>
ConditionalExpression[-21.04+2.5 Log[t]+0[[1]]/t,Re[t]>=0||t∉Reals]
-18.5169+2.5 Log[t]
(* Enthalpy functions at 1 bar *)
(* Each is in Sv. *)
(* In the following equations, the lower limits of the integrals are T=298.15K--
the temperature at which McBride2002 sets the enthalpy to be equal to the enthalpy of formation. *)
h0[theta2_]:=Integrate[cp0[theta2],theta2]
h0eminus[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0eminus[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/meminus,theta2}]+hf0eminus[[1]]]
h0H[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0H[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mH,theta2}]+hf0H[[1]]]
h0Hplus[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0Hplus[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mHplus,theta2}]+hf0Hplus[[1]]]
h0Hminus[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0Hminus[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mHminus,theta2}]+hf0Hminus[[1]]]
h0H2[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0H2[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mH2,theta2}]+hf0H2[[1]]]
h0H2O[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0H2O[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mH2O,theta2}]+hf0H2O[[1]]]
h0H2Ol[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0H2Ol[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mH2O,theta2}]+hf0H2Ol[[1]]]
h0H3Oplus[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0H3Oplus[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mH3Oplus,theta2}]+hf0H3Oplus[[1]]]
h0O2[theta2_]:=Expand[Integrate[cp0O2[theta2int],{theta2int,298.15UK/mO2,theta2}]+hf0O2[[1]]]
(* **The results above and below don't match for Subscript[H, 2]O liquid or gas.  Why? *)
(* For computational efficiency, the lower limits of the integrals are pre-subtracted from hf0, and the results are saved as b[[2]].  That allows the equations to be written in the following equivalent form--McBride2002, p. 2, eq. 3. *)
h0eminus[theta2_]:=-aeminus[[1]]theta2^-1+aeminus[[2]]Log[theta2]+aeminus[[3]]theta2+aeminus[[4]]theta2^2/2+aeminus[[5]]theta2^3/3+aeminus[[6]]theta2^4/4+aeminus[[7]]theta2^5/5+beminus[[1]]
h0H[theta2_]:=-aH[[1]]theta2^-1+aH[[2]]Log[theta2]+aH[[3]]theta2+aH[[4]]theta2^2/2+aH[[5]]theta2^3/3+aH[[6]]theta2^4/4+aH[[7]]theta2^5/5+bH[[1]]
h0Hplus[theta2_]:=-aHplus[[1]]theta2^-1+aHplus[[2]]Log[theta2]+aHplus[[3]]theta2+aHplus[[4]]theta2^2/2+aHplus[[5]]theta2^3/3+aHplus[[6]]theta2^4/4+aHplus[[7]]theta2^5/5+bHplus[[1]]
h0Hminus[theta2_]:=-aHminus[[1]]theta2^-1+aHminus[[2]]Log[theta2]+aHminus[[3]]theta2+aHminus[[4]]theta2^2/2+aHminus[[5]]theta2^3/3+aHminus[[6]]theta2^4/4+aHminus[[7]]theta2^5/5+bHminus[[1]]
h0H2[theta2_]:=-aH2[[1]]theta2^-1+aH2[[2]]Log[theta2]+aH2[[3]]theta2+aH2[[4]]theta2^2/2+aH2[[5]]theta2^3/3+aH2[[6]]theta2^4/4+aH2[[7]]theta2^5/5+bH2[[1]]
h0H2O[theta2_]:=-aH2O[[1]]theta2^-1+aH2O[[2]]Log[theta2]+aH2O[[3]]theta2+aH2O[[4]]theta2^2/2+aH2O[[5]]theta2^3/3+aH2O[[6]]theta2^4/4+aH2O[[7]]theta2^5/5+bH2O[[1]]
h0H2Ol[theta2_]:=-aH2Ol[[1]]theta2^-1+aH2Ol[[2]]Log[theta2]+aH2Ol[[3]]theta2+aH2Ol[[4]]theta2^2/2+aH2Ol[[5]]theta2^3/3+aH2Ol[[6]]theta2^4/4+aH2Ol[[7]]theta2^5/5+bH2Ol[[1]]
h0H3Oplus[theta2_]:=-aH3Oplus[[1]]theta2^-1+aH3Oplus[[2]]Log[theta2]+aH3Oplus[[3]]theta2+aH3Oplus[[4]]theta2^2/2+aH3Oplus[[5]]theta2^3/3+aH3Oplus[[6]]theta2^4/4+aH3Oplus[[7]]theta2^5/5+bH3Oplus[[1]]
h0O2[theta2_]:=-aO2[[1]]theta2^-1+aO2[[2]]Log[theta2]+aO2[[3]]theta2+aO2[[4]]theta2^2/2+aO2[[5]]theta2^3/3+aO2[[6]]theta2^4/4+aO2[[7]]theta2^5/5+bO2[[1]]
(* Gibbs functions at 1 bar *)
(* Each is in Sv. *)
g0[theta2_]:=Expand[h0[theta2]-theta2*s0[theta2]]
g0eminus[theta2_]:=Expand[h0eminus[theta2]-theta2*s0eminus[theta2]]
g0H[theta2_]:=Expand[h0H[theta2]-theta2*s0H[theta2]]
g0Hplus[theta2_]:=Expand[h0Hplus[theta2]-theta2*s0Hplus[theta2]]
g0Hminus[theta2_]:=Expand[h0Hminus[theta2]-theta2*s0Hminus[theta2]]
g0H2[theta2_]:=Expand[h0H2[theta2]-theta2*s0H2[theta2]]
g0H2O[theta2_]:=Expand[h0H2O[theta2]-theta2*s0H2O[theta2]]
g0H2Ol[theta2_]:=Expand[h0H2Ol[theta2]-theta2*s0H2Ol[theta2]]
g0H3Oplus[theta2_]:=Expand[h0H3Oplus[theta2]-theta2*s0H3Oplus[theta2]]
g0O2[theta2_]:=Expand[h0O2[theta2]-theta2*s0O2[theta2]]
(* Internal energy functions at 1 bar *)
(* Each is in Sv. *)
u0[theta2_]:=h0[theta2]-1
u0eminus[theta2_]:=h0eminus[theta2]-1
u0H[theta2_]:=h0H[theta2]-1
u0Hplus[theta2_]:=h0Hplus[theta2]-1
u0Hminus[theta2_]:=h0Hminus[theta2]-1
u0H2[theta2_]:=h0H2[theta2]-1
u0H2O[theta2_]:=h0H2O[theta2]-1
u0H2Ol[theta2_]:=h0H2Ol[theta2]-1
u0H3Oplus[theta2_]:=h0H3Oplus[theta2]-1
u0O2[theta2_]:=h0O2[theta2]-1
(* Helmholtz functions at 1 bar *)
(* Each is in Sv. *)
a0[theta2_]:=Expand[u0[theta2]-theta2*s0[theta2]]
a0eminus[theta2_]:=Expand[u0eminus[theta2]-theta2*s0eminus[theta2]]
a0H[theta2_]:=Expand[u0H[theta2]-theta2*s0H[theta2]]
a0Hplus[theta2_]:=Expand[u0Hplus[theta2]-theta2*s0Hplus[theta2]]
a0Hminus[theta2_]:=Expand[u0Hminus[theta2]-theta2*s0Hminus[theta2]]
a0H2[theta2_]:=Expand[u0H2[theta2]-theta2*s0H2[theta2]]
a0H2O[theta2_]:=Expand[u0H2O[theta2]-theta2*s0H2O[theta2]]
a0H2Ol[theta2_]:=Expand[u0H2Ol[theta2]-theta2*s0H2Ol[theta2]]
a0H3Oplus[theta2_]:=Expand[u0H3Oplus[theta2]-theta2*s0H3Oplus[theta2]]
a0O2[theta2_]:=Expand[u0O2[theta2]-theta2*s0O2[theta2]]
(* List the thermodynamic functions. *)
cp0[theta2]
s0[theta2]
h0[theta2]
g0[theta2]
a0[theta2]
u0[theta2]
a3+a1/theta2^2+a2/theta2+a4 theta2+a5 theta2^2+a6 theta2^3+a7 theta2^4
-(a1/(2 theta2^2))-a2/theta2+a4 theta2+(a5 theta2^2)/2+(a6 theta2^3)/3+(a7 theta2^4)/4+a3 Log[theta2]
-(a1/theta2)+a3 theta2+(a4 theta2^2)/2+(a5 theta2^3)/3+(a6 theta2^4)/4+(a7 theta2^5)/5+a2 Log[theta2]
a2-a1/(2 theta2)+a3 theta2-(a4 theta2^2)/2-(a5 theta2^3)/6-(a6 theta2^4)/12-(a7 theta2^5)/20+a2 Log[theta2]-a3 theta2 Log[theta2]
-1+a2-a1/(2 theta2)+a3 theta2-(a4 theta2^2)/2-(a5 theta2^3)/6-(a6 theta2^4)/12-(a7 theta2^5)/20+a2 Log[theta2]-a3 theta2 Log[theta2]
-1-a1/theta2+a3 theta2+(a4 theta2^2)/2+(a5 theta2^3)/3+(a6 theta2^4)/4+(a7 theta2^5)/5+a2 Log[theta2]
(* Heat capacity at 1 bar vs. temperature *)

(* Subscript[H, 2]/Subscript[O, 2] cell potential at 1 atm *)
DeltaepsilonRev[T_]:=(2*mH2*h0H2[T/mH2]+mO2*h0O2[T/mO2]-2*mH2O*h0H2O[T/mH2O]+T*Log[101.325/100])/4 (* Reversible with Subscript[H, 2] Subscript[O, (g)], assuming IG *)
DeltaepsilonRevl[T_]:=(2*mH2*h0H2[T/mH2]+mO2*h0O2[T/mO2]-2*mH2O*h0H2Ol[T/mH2O]+3*T*Log[101.325/100])/4 (* Reversible with Subscript[H, 2] Subscript[O, (l)], assuming IG; **adjust for liquid Subscript[H, 2]O at 1atm rather than 1bar--v*dp of liquid water using water density function.  Subtract: 2*(101325-1000000)*UPa/Nprime3[T/mH2O]. *)
DeltaepsilonIso[T_]:=(2*mH2*g0H2[T/mH2]+mO2*g0O2[T/mO2]-2*mH2O*g0H2O[T/mH2O]+T*Log[101.325/100])/4 (* Isothermal with Subscript[H, 2] Subscript[O, (g)], assuming IG *)
DeltaepsilonIsol[T_]:=(2*mH2*g0H2[T/mH2]+mO2*g0O2[T/mO2]-2*mH2O*g0H2Ol[T/mH2O]+3*T*Log[101.325/100])/4 (* Isothermal with Subscript[H, 2] Subscript[O, (l)], assuming IG; **adjust for liquid Subscript[H, 2]O at 1atm rather than 1bar--v*dp of liquid water using water density function.  Subtract: 2*(101325-1000000)*UPa/Nprime3[T/mH2O]. *)
LineLegendFromTooltips[Plot[{Tooltip[DeltaepsilonRev[T*UK]/UV,"Reversible"],Tooltip[DeltaepsilonIso[T*UK]/UV,"Isothermal"]},{T,200,1000},
PlotLabel->Style["Subscript[H, 2]/Subscript[O, 2] Cell Potential at 1 atm with Subscript[H, 2]O as Gas",FontSize->13],
FrameLabel->{"Temperature / K","Potential / V"}]]


GraphicsBox[
{RGBColor[0, 1, 0], Thickness[0.06], LineBox[{{0, 0}, {1, 0}}]},
AspectRatio->NCache[Rational[1, 3], 0.3333333333333333],
ImagePadding->0,
ImageSize->{24, 8}]	Isothermal






(* Subscript[H, 2]O saturation pressure *)
psat[theta2_]:=100000Exp[(g0H2Ol[theta2]-g0H2O[theta2])/theta2]; (* Pa; using Gibbs energy of formation via McBride2002, which uses reference pressure of 100 kPa *)
psatMod[theta2_]:=611.657Exp[17.2799-4102.99/(mH2O*theta2/UK-35.719)]; (* Pa; from Modelica.Media.Air.MoistAir; valid for 273.16K <= T <= 373.16K; Outside this range, a less accurate result is returned. *)
psatSpr[theta2_]:=101325Exp[Log[10](-20.04328416+0.112053341mH2O*theta2/UK-0.00021028(mH2O*theta2/UK)^2+1.4454*^-7(mH2O*theta2/UK)^3)];(* Pa; from Eq. 15 in (Springer et al. 1991); more accurate than equation above over entire range 273.16K <= T <= 423.16K; However, it is more complicated, and 273.16K <= T <= 373.16K is sufficient for PEMFC use. *)
tau[theta2_]:=1-mH2O*theta2/UK/647.096
psatKaytau[tau_]:=22064*^3Exp[(((1.80122502tau^3.5-15.9618719)tau+22.6807411Sqrt[tau]-11.7866497)tau^2+1.84408259Sqrt[tau]-7.85951783)tau/(1-tau)] (* Pa; Kaye and Laby Online, 2005 *)
psatKay[T_]:=psatKaytau[tau[T]] (* Pa; Kaye & Laby Online, 2005 *)
LineLegendFromTooltips[Plot[{Tooltip[psat[T*UK/mH2O]/1000,"via Gibbs function"],Tooltip[psatMod[T*UK/mH2O]/1000,"Modelica"],Tooltip[psatSpr[T*UK/mH2O]/1000,"Springer et al. 1991"],Tooltip[psatKay[T*UK/mH2O]/1000,"Kaye & Laby Online, 2005"]},{T,273.15,373.15},
PlotLabel->Style["Subscript[H, 2]O Saturation Pressure",FontSize->13],
FrameLabel->{"Temperature / K","Pressure / kPa"}]]

(* Subscript[H, 2]O gas EOS *)
CIG[P_,T_]:=P/(R*T)
f[T_]:=1*^-6*(33-15.2*Exp[1300.7/T]) (* Ideal gas *)
CKay[P_,T_]:=(-0.5+Sqrt[0.25+f[T]*P/(R*T)])/f[T] (* Kaye & Laby Online, 2005 *)
LineLegendFromTooltips[Plot[{Tooltip[CIG[100000,T],"Ideal gas @ 1 bar"],Tooltip[CIG[500000,T],"Ideal gas @ 5 bar"],Tooltip[CKay[100000,T],"Kaye & Laby Online, 2005 @ 1 bar"],Tooltip[CKay[500000,T],"Kaye & Laby Online, 2005 @ 5 bar"]},{T,200,1000},
PlotLabel->Style["Subscript[H, 2]O Gas Concentration",FontSize->13],
FrameLabel->{"Temperature / K","Concentration / mol m^-3"}]]
